```markdown
MEMORANDUM OF UNDERSTANDING ON ACADEMIC AND RESEARCH

決議：是否通過本提案？

## AGREEMENT FOREDUCATIONAL COOPERATIONBETWEENYUAN ZE UNIVERSITYANDTOMSK STATE UNIVERSITY

In order to promote international educational cooperation and educational exchanges, Yuan Ze University and Tomsk State University join in the following agreement on educational cooperation.

Both universities will endeavor to cooperate in joint educational programs and research projects. To the extent feasible, both universities will encourage direct contact and cooperation between their faculty members, departments, and research institutes under provisions of this agreement.

Within fields that are mutually acceptable, the following general forms of cooperation will be pursued:

1. Collaboration of faculty and staff for research, lectures, discussions and other academic pursuits.

2. Reciprocal exchange of undergraduate or graduate students for study and research.

3. Exchange of published information.

Arrangements for specific visits, dual degree programs, and other forms of cooperation will be developed jointly and will be agreed upon for each specific case. No monetary consideration will be exchanged between the institutions. Both parties understand all financial arrangements will have to be negotiated and will depend on the availability of funds.

This agreement will become valid upon signed by the appropriate officials of the two institutions. This agreement shall remain in effect until one party notifies the other of its intention to terminate this agreement in writing at least ninety (90) days before the end of the academic year.

IN WITNESS WHEREFORE, this document has been executed on

Yuan Ze University

Tomsk State University

By:

By:

Jyh-Yang, Wu, Ph.D.

Eduard Galazhinskiy, Professor

President

Rector

Yuan Ze University

Tomsk State University

135 Yuan-Tung Road, Chung-Li District,

Lenin Avenue 36, 634050 Tomsk, Russia

# AGREEMENT REGARDING STUDENT EXCHANGE PROGRAMS BETWEEN YUAN ZE UNIVERSITY AND TOMSK STATE UNIVERSITY

This Agreement is made as of (date) by and between Yuan Ze University, Chung-Li, Taiwan, R.O.C., (hereinafter “YZU”) and Tomsk State University, Tomsk, Russia (hereinafter “TSU”) pursuant to the Cooperation Agreement executed between the two universities.

The purpose of this Agreement is to establish the terms and conditions under which the exchange of students between YZU and TSU shall take place.

Both parties hereby agree that:

## 1. Program Management

The student exchange program shall be available to students of both universities and shall be administered by YZU and TSU respectively via the Office of International Affairs of YZU and Centre for Joint Academic Programmes of TSU.

## 2. Exchange Student Numbers

The maximum number of students nominated for exchange in one (1) given academic year is 4 (four).

## 3. Exchange Period

The normal period of exchange for each exchange student shall be one (1) or two (2) consecutive semesters with the consent of both universities.

## 4. Admission Requirements

Exchange candidates must have completed at least one (1) academic year of study at the home university prior to the exchange period, with an overall GPA of 2.5 or higher out of a 4.0 grade scale for YZU students, and 4.0 or higher out of 5.0 for TSU students. Each party will notify the other as quickly as possible if any changes are made to student exchange admission requirements. While it is understood that exchange candidates nominated by the home university will normally be accepted by the host university, the host university reserves the right to review the applications of nominees and make final decisions concerning their admission.

## 5. Language Requirements

Nominees must obtain a TOEFL score of 500 and present proof of the score when applying. Language requirements can also be equivalent but is certified by the Language Center. Each party will notify the other as quickly as possible if any changes are made to language requirements.

## 6. Application Documents

YZU will forward the appropriate application documents to TSU by November 15 for spring admission, and April 15 for fall semester admission, of each year. TSU will inform YZU of its final admission decision within thirty (30) days after the application deadline. TSU will forward to YZU by November 15 for spring admission, and April 15 for fall semester admission, of each year, the appropriate documents as required by YZU. YZU will inform TSU of its final admission decision within thirty (30) days after the application deadline.

## 7. Visa

The host university will issue appropriate documents to accepted students for visa purposes in accordance with their respective applicable laws and regulations. It is the responsibility of the individual exchange student to obtain a visa in a timely manner.

## 8. Courses

Exchange students will be able to take courses regularly offered at the host university and will have all the rights and privileges enjoyed by other students at that university.

## 9. Credit Transfer

Any academic credit received during the course of the program may be transferred to the home university in accordance with the appropriate regulations of the home university. The host university will inform the home university of exchange students’ grade information in a timely manner upon the request of the exchange student or the home university.

## 10. Tuition and Fees

Exchange students will pay normal tuition and fees to their home university in accordance with the policies of that university. The host university will not charge the home university or the exchange students for application, admission fees and tuition. Notwithstanding the number of the exchange student, neither party assumes any payment obligation to the other party in connection with this Agreement.

## 11. Miscellaneous Fees

Exchange students will be responsible for making their international travel arrangements and shall bear all associated costs, including but not limited to, room, board, study materials, local transportation, student health insurance and medical care, personal expenses, and passport/visa application fees. Regarding payment of these expenses, the home university, together with the host university, shall assume responsibility for providing guidance and dealing with situations that may arise so as not to cause undue inconvenience to third parties when exchange students fall into arrears.

## 12. Liability

During their time at the host university, exchange students will be individually liable for any and all incidents, accidents and damage to third parties resulting from the students’ actions where these actions occur in situations beyond the control of the host university and home university. Both parties will not hold each other liable for such incidents.

## 13. Insurance

It is mandatory for exchange students from both institutes to purchase overseas travel insurance before departure.

## 14. Accommodation

The host university will assume responsibility for finding suitable accommodation for exchange students. The cost of the accommodation shall be borne by the individual exchange student.

## 15. Student Support

The host university will make every effort to facilitate integration of exchange students into the student life of the host university. The host university will strive to protect the privacy of the student as well as their personal safety in addition to offering orientation sessions and a sufficient support network for everyday life.

## 16. Emergency Procedures

Both the host university and the home university shall provide the other with emergency contact information and will be responsible for carrying out emergency notification in the event of student illness, injury, or other emergencies.

## 17. Appropriate Use of Personal Information

When obtaining personal information from the exchange student, it is necessary for both the host university and the home university to inform the student ahead of time of the purposes for its use and to keep its use to a minimum. Personal information must be managed carefully to prevent its spread to a third party or use for purposes unauthorized by the exchange student.

## 18. Rules and Regulations

Exchange students shall be subject to the rules and regulations of the host university. Each university reserves the right to dismiss any exchange student at any time for conduct in violation of their established rules and regulations. However, the dismissal of an exchange student shall not adversely affect the agreement and the arrangements regarding other exchange students.

## 19. Length of Stay

Upon completion of the program at the host university, exchange students are required to return to the home university. No extension of stay will be authorized unless otherwise specifically agreed upon by both universities.

## 20. Negotiations

Both parties will strive to resolve any misunderstandings out of or in relation to this agreement that arise in a sincere and respectful manner.

## 21. Agreement Period

This Agreement shall remain in effect from the date of execution for an initial period of five (5) years. Unless either party notifies the other in writing to terminate the Agreement at least six (6) months prior to the date of expiration, the Agreement will be automatically renewed and extended for another five (5) years from the date of expiration. In the case of termination, both universities shall make necessary arrangements to ensure the appropriate completion of ongoing exchanges. This Agreement may be amended by mutual written consent the two of universities through consultation.

The parties hereto have caused this Agreement written in 4 copies: 2 in English and 2 in Russian, to be executed in duplicate by their duly authorized representatives as of the date first above written, with each party retaining one original. Each copy is of the same validity and each is recognized as official.

Jyh-Yang, Wu, Ph.D.

Eduard Galazhiskiy

President

Rector

Yuan Ze University

Tomsk State University

Date

Date
```

```markdown
## 【討論案十】

提案單 位：全球事務處

案由名稱：元智大學與興義民族師範學院簽訂「學術合作與交流意向書」暨「人才培育合作意向書」審議案

提案說明：

## 一、興義民族師範學院

興義民族師範學院肇始於 1813年重建的筆山書院，於 1952年更名為貴州省興義師範學校，開始了現代師範教育的歷史。1975年時，更名為興義地區「五七」師範大學，幾經更迭而於2009年3月經教育部批准，正式升格為興義民族師範學院，成為一所「省州共建、以州為主」的地方性日間部專招大學部學生的大學校院。

該校位於黔滇桂三省（區），南鄰廣西，西接雲南，地處珠江上游和南昆鐵路中段，即黔西南州州府所在地－興義市。現有在職教職工 640人，師資隊伍469人，其中正高職稱 26人、博士11人；有省級教學名師 1人、青年“千人計畫”入選者4人；有省級高層次研究團隊 1個。學校現有 14個二級學院，27個本科專業（其中新專業 22個）、11個專科專業和 1個少數民族雙語預科班；專業涵蓋了文學、理學、工學、法學、教育學、管理學、歷史學、藝術學八大學科門類；有3個省級重點支持學科、一個省級實驗室和一個省級科研基地；有 16個校內科研機構（中心）。學校現有 14個二級學院，27個本科專業（其中新專業22個）、11個專科專業和 1個少數民族雙語預科班；專業涵蓋了文學、理學、工學、法學、教育學、管理學、歷史學、藝術學八大學科門類；有 3 個省級重點支持學科、一個省級實驗室和一個省級科研基地；有 16個校內科研機構（中心）。

學校占地 78.32 萬平方尺（1,175畝），校舍建築總面積 23.27 萬平方公尺，其中教學行政用房 10.74萬平方公尺，學生宿舍 7.89萬平方公尺；館藏圖書 63.8萬冊，電子圖書74.1 萬種；教學科研儀器設備總值 4,682.98萬元。

該校已獲國家自然科學基金專案 2項、國家哲學社會科學基金專案 2項；獲省社科規劃課題6項、省科學技術基金專案 25項、省長基金資助專案 9項、地廳級專案立項162項；獲貴州省科學技術進步獎二等獎 1項、貴州省哲學社會科學優秀成果獎三等獎 2 項、黔西南州科學技術進步獎三等獎 3 項。教師共發表論文 1843 篇，其中中文核心期刊及 CSSCI 收錄論文共 264 篇，SCI、EI、ISSHP等國際權威學術文獻收錄 23篇；出版教材和著作 25部；建有貴州省黔西南特色產業扶貧與生態修復協同創新中心 1個。

該校排名狀況與先前簽約種類與狀態：

## 一、興義師範學院

1. 中國校友網 2017 年排名：大陸西南地區城市大學競爭力排名第27 名，全國第222名，2017黔西南布依族苗族自治州最好大学排行榜師範類型第 657名。

提案程序：4月17 日會簽一級主管提請105 學年度第17次行政會議審議。

會簽意見：無

檢附資料：

決議：是否通過本提案？
```
